  142→\n   143→// New makes a new Client.\n   144→func New(reg prometheus.Registerer, cfg Config, logger log.Logger) (Client, error) {\n   145→\treturn newClient(reg, cfg, logger)\n   146→}\n   147→\n   148→func newClient(reg prometheus.Registerer, cfg Config, logger log.Logger) (*client, error) {\n   149→\tif cfg.URL.URL == nil {\n   150→\t\treturn nil, errors.New(\"client needs target URL\")\n   151→\t}\n   152→\n   153→\tctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(context.Background())\n   154→\n   155→\tc := &client{\n   156→\t\tlogger:  logger.New(\"host\", cfg.URL.Host),\n   157→\t\tcfg:     cfg,\n   158→\t\tentries: make(chan Entry),\n   159→\t\tmetrics: newMetrics(reg),\n   160→\n   161→\t\tctx:    ctx,\n   162→\t\tcancel: cancel,\n   163→\t}\n   164→\n   165→\terr := cfg.Client.Validate()\n   166→\tif err != nil {\n   167→\t\treturn nil, err\n   168→\t}\n   169→\n   170→\tc.client, err = config.NewClientFromConfig(cfg.Client, \"promtail\", config.WithHTTP2Disabled())\n   171→\tif err != 183→\tc.wg.Add(1)\n   184→\tgo c.run()\n   185→\treturn c, nil\n   186→}\n   187→\n   188→// NewWithTripperware creates a new Loki client with a custom tripperware.\n   189→func NewWithTripperware(reg 193→\t}\n   194→\n   195→\tif tp != nil {\n   196→\t\tc.client.Transport = tp(c.client.Transport)\n   197→\t}\n   198→\n   199→\treturn c, nil\n   200→}\n   201→\n   202→func (c *client) run() {\n   203→\tbatches := map[string]*batch{}\n   204→\n   205→\t// Given the client handles multiple batches (1 per tenant) and each batch\n   206→\t// can be created at a different point in time, we look for batches whose\n   207→\t// max wait time has been reached every 10 times per BatchWait, so that the\n   208→\t// maximum delay we have sending batches is 10% of the max waiting time.\n   209→\t// We apply a cap of 10ms to the ticker, to avoid too frequent checks in\n   210→\t// case the BatchWait is very low.\n   211→\tminWaitCheckFrequency := 10 * time.Millisecond\n   212→\tmaxWaitCheckFrequency := c.cfg.BatchWait / 10\n   213→\tif maxWaitCheckFrequency < minWaitCheckFrequency {\n   214→\t\tmaxWaitCheckFrequency = minWaitCheckFrequency\n   215→\t}\n   216→\n   217→\tmaxWaitCheck := time.NewTicker(maxWaitCheckFrequency)\n   218→\n   219→\tdefer func() {\n   220→\t\tmaxWaitCheck.Stop()\n   221→\t\t// Send all pending batches\n   222→\t\tfor tenantID, batch := range batches {\n lokiError\n   122→\terr := json.Unmarshal(bytes, &data)\n   123→\tif err != nil {\n   124→\t\t// we were unable to convert the bytes to JSON, we return the whole text\n   125→\t\treturn getSupportingQueryHeaderValue(supportingQueryType SupportingQueryType) string {\n   322→\tvalue := \"\"\n   323→\n   324→\t// we need to map the SupportingQueryType to the actual header value. For\n   325→\t// legacy reasons we defined each value, such as \"logsVolume\" maps to the\n   326→\t// \"logvolhist\" header value to Loki. Header not set\")\n   355→\t\treturn req\n   356→\t}\n   357→\n   358→\ttenantids := md.Get(\"tenantid\")\n   359→\tif len(tenantids) == 0 {\n   360→\t\t// We assume we are not using multi-tenant mode, which is fine\n   361→\t\tlogger.Debug(\"Tenant ID not present. Header not set\")\n   362→\t} else if len(tenantids) > 1 {\n   363→\t\t// Loki supports multiple tenant IDs, but we should receive them from different contexts\n   364→\t\tlogger.Error(strconv.Itoa(len(tenantids)) + \" tenant IDs found. Header not set\")\n   365→\t} else {\n   366→\t\treq.Header.Add(\"X-Scope-OrgID\", tenantids[0])\n   367→\t\tlogger.Debug(\"Tenant ID \" + tenantids[0] + \" added to Loki request\")\n   368→\t}\n   369→\treturn req\n   370→}\n   371→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. makeDataRequest(ctx context.Context, lokiDsUrl string, query lokiQuery) (*http.Request, error) {\n\tqs := url.Values{}\n\tqs.Set(\"query\", query.Expr)\n\n\tqs.Set(\"direction\", send it when it's set\n\tif query.MaxLines > 0 {\n\t\tqs.Set(\"limit\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%d\", query.MaxLines))\n\t}\n\n\tlokiUrl, err := url.Parse(lokiDsUrl)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, strconv.FormatInt(query.Start.UnixNano(), 10))\n\t\t\tqs.Set(\"end\", strconv.FormatInt(query.End.UnixNano(), 10))\n\t\t\t// NOTE: technically for streams-producing queries `step`\n\t\t\t// is ignored, so it would be nicer to not send it in such cases,\n\t\t\t// but we cannot detect that situation, so we always send it.\n\t\t\t// it should not break anything.\n\t\t\t// NOTE2: we do this at millisecond precision for two reasons:\n\t\t\t//  a. Loki cannot do steps with better precision anyway,\n\t\t\t//     so the microsecond & nanosecond part can be ignored.\n\t\t\t//  b. having it always be number+'ms' makes it more robust and\n\t\t\t//     precise, as Loki does not support step with float number\n\t\t\t//     and time-specifier, like \"1.5s\"\n\t\t\tqs.Set(\"step\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%dms\", query.Step.Milliseconds()))\n\t\t\tlokiUrl.Path = path.Join(lokiUrl.Path, \"/loki/api/v1/query_range\")\n\t\t}\n\tcase QueryTypeInstant:\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tqs.Set(\"time\", strconv.FormatInt(query.End.UnixNano(), 10))\n\t\t\tlokiUrl.Path = path.Join(lokiUrl.Path, \"/loki/api/v1/query\")\n\t\t}\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn nil, backend.DownstreamError(fmt.Errorf(\"invalid QueryType: %v\", query.QueryType))\n\t}\n\n\tlokiUrl.RawQuery = makeLokiError(bytes []byte) error {\n\tvar data lokiError\n\terr := json.Unmarshal(bytes, &data)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\t// we were unable to convert the bytes to JSON, we return the whole text\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"%v\", string(bytes))\n\t}\n\n\tif data.Message == \"\" {\n\t\t// we got no usable error message, we return the whole text\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"%v\", string(bytes))\n\t}\n\n\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"%v\", data.Message)\n}\n\n// we know there is an error,\n// based on the http-response-body\n// we have to make an informative error-object\nfunc readLokiError(body io.ReadCloser) error {\n\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\n\t_, err := buf.ReadFrom(body)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\tbytes := buf.Bytes()\n\n\t// the error-message is probably a JSON structure,\n\t// with a string-field named \"message\". we want the\n\t// value of that field.\n\t// but, the response might be just a simple string,\n\t// this was used in older Loki versions.\n\t// so our approach is this:\n\t// - we try to convert the bytes to JSON\n\t// - we take the value of the field \"message\"\n\t// - if any of these steps fail, or if \"message\" is empty, we return the whole text\n\n\treturn makeLokiError(bytes)\n}\n\nfunc (api *LokiAPI) DataQuery(ctx context.Context, query lokiQuery, responseOpts ResponseOpts) (*backend.DataResponse, error) {\n\treq, With #85123, even the value set in the\n\t// frontend query can be passed as is to Loki.\n\tswitch supportingQueryType {\n\tcase SupportingQueryLogsVolume:\n\t\tvalue = \"logvolhist\"\n\tcase SupportingQueryLogsSample:\n\t\tvalue = \"logsample\"\n\tcase SupportingQueryDataSample:\n\t\tvalue = \"datasample\"\n\tcase SupportingQueryInfiniteScroll:\n\t\tvalue = \"infinitescroll\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\tvalue = string(supportingQueryType)\n\t}\n\n\treturn value\n}\n\n// setXScopeOrgIDHeader sets the `X-Scope-OrgID` header in the provided HTTP request based on the tenant ID retrieved from the context.\n// `X-Scope-OrgID` is needed by the Loki system to work in multi-tenant mode.\n// See https://github.com/grafana/loki/blob/main/docs/sources/operations/multi-tenancy.md\nfunc setXScopeOrgIDHeader(req *http.Request, ctx context.Context) *http.Request {\n\tlogger := backend.NewLoggerWith(\"logger\", \"tsdb.loki\")\n\n\tmd, ok := metadata.FromIncomingContext(ctx)\n\tif !ok {\n\t\t// Metadata are currently set and needed only locally for multi-tenancy, while on cloud\n\t\t// this is set by our stack\n\t\tlogger.Debug(\"Metadata not present in context. Header not set\")\n\t\treturn req\n\t}\n\n\ttenantids := md.Get(\"tenantid\")\n\tif len(tenantids) == 0 {\n\t\t// We assume we are not using multi-tenant mode, which is fine\n\t\tlogger.Debug(\"Tenant ID not present. Header not set\")\n\t} else if len(tenantids) > 1 {\n\t\t// Loki supports multiple tenant IDs, but we should receive them from different contexts\n\t\tlogger.Error(strconv.Itoa(len(tenantids)) + \" tenant IDs found. Header not set\")\n\t} else {\n\t\treq.Header.Add(\"X-Scope-OrgID\", tenantids[0])\n\t\tlogger.Debug(\"Tenant ID \" + tenantids[0] + \" added to Loki request\")\n\t}\n\treturn req\n}\n","numLines":371,"startLine":1,"totalLines":371}}}

46→func makeDataRequest(ctx context.Context, lokiDsUrl string, query lokiQuery) (*http.Request, error) {\n    47→\tqs := url.Values{}\n    48→\tqs.Set(\"query\", query.Expr)\n    49→\n    50→\tqs.Set(\"direction\", string(query.Direction))\n    51→\n    52→\t// MaxLines defaults to zero when not received,\n    53→\t// and Loki does not like limit=0, even when it is not needed\n    54→\t// (for example for metric queries), so we\n    55→\t// only send it when it's set\n    56→\tif query.MaxLines > 0 {\n    57→\t\tqs.Set(\"limit\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%d\", query.MaxLines))\n    58→\t}\n    59→\n    60→\tlokiUrl, err := url.Parse(lokiDsUrl)\n    61→\tif err != nil {\n    62→\t\treturn nil, backend.DownstreamError(fmt.Errorf(\"failed to parse Loki URL: %w\", err))\n    63→\t}\n    64→\n    65→\tswitch query.QueryType {\n    66→\tcase QueryTypeRange:\n    67→\t\t{\n    68→\t\t\tqs.Set(\"start\", strconv.FormatInt(query.Start.UnixNano(), 10))\n    69→\t\t\tqs.Set(\"end\", strconv.FormatInt(query.End.UnixNano(), 10))\n    70→\t\t\t// NOTE: technically for streams-producing queries `step`\n    71→\t\t\t// is ignored, so it would be nicer to not send it in such cases,\n    72→\t\t\t// but we cannot detect that situation, so we always send it.\n    73→\t\t\t// it should not break anything.\n    74→\t\t\t// NOTE2: we do this at millisecond precision for two reasons:\n    75→\t\t\t//  a. Loki cannot do steps with better precision anyway,\n    76→\t\t\t//     so the microsecond & nanosecond part can be ignored.\n    77→\t\t\t//  b. having it always be number+'ms' makes it more robust 85→\t\t\tqs.Set(\"time\", strconv.FormatInt(query.End.UnixNano(), 10))\n    86→\t\t\tlokiUrl.Path = path.Join(lokiUrl.Path, \"/loki/api/v1/query\")\n    87→\t\t}\n    88→\tdefault:\n    89→\t\treturn 97→\t}\n    98→\n    99→\tif query.SupportingQueryType != SupportingQueryNone {\n   100→\t\tvalue := getSupportingQueryHeaderValue(query.SupportingQueryType)\n   101→\t\tif value != \"\" {\n   102→\t\t\treq.Header.Set(\"X-Query-Tags\", \"Source=\"+value)\n   103→\t\t}\n   104→\t}\n   105→\treq.Header.Set(\"X-Loki-Response-Encoding-Flags\", \"categorize-labels\")\n   106→\tsetXScopeOrgIDHeader(req, ctx)\n   107→\n   108→\treturn req, nil\n   109→}\n   110→\n   111→type lokiResponseError struct {\n   112→\tMessage string `json:\"message\"`\n   113→\tTraceID string `json:\"traceID,omitempty\"`\n   114→}\n   115→\n   116→type lokiError struct {\n   117→\tMessage string\n   118→}\n   119→\n   120→func makeLokiError(bytes []byte) error {\n   121→\tvar data lokiError\n   122→\terr := json.Unmarshal(bytes, &data)\n   123→\tif err != nil {\n   124→\t\t// we were unable to convert the bytes to JSON, we return the whole text\n   125→\t\treturn string(bytes))\n   131→\t}\n   132→\n   133→\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"%v\", data.Message)\n   134→}\n   135→\n   136→// we know there is an error,\n   137→// based on the http-response-body\n   138→// we have to make an informative error-object\n   139→func readLokiError(body io.ReadCloser) error {\n   140→\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\n   141→\t_, err := buf.ReadFrom(body)\n   142→\tif err != nil {\n   143→\t\treturn err\n   144→\t}\n   145→\n   146→\tbytes := buf.Bytes()\n   147→\n   148→\t// the error-message is probably a JSON structure,\n   149→\t// with a string-field named \"message\". we want the\n   150→\t// value of that field.\n   151→\t// but, the response might be just a simple string,\n   152→\t// this was used in older Loki versions.\n   153→\t// so our approach is this:\n   154→\t// - we try to convert the bytes to JSON\n   155→\t// - we take the value of the field \"message\"\n   156→\t// - if any of these steps fail, or if \"message\" is empty, we return the whole text\n   157→\n   158→\treturn makeLokiError(bytes)\n   159→}\n   160→\n   161→func (api *LokiAPI) DataQuery(ctx context.Context, query lokiQuery, responseOpts ResponseOpts) (*backend.DataResponse, 46→func makeDataRequest(ctx context.Context, lokiDsUrl string, query lokiQuery) (*http.Request, error) {\n    47→\tqs := url.Values{}\n    48→\tqs.Set(\"query\", query.Expr)\n    49→\n    50→\tqs.Set(\"direction\", string(query.Direction))\n    51→\n    52→\t// MaxLines defaults to zero when not received,\n    53→\t// and Loki does not like limit=0, even when it is not needed\n    54→\t// (for example for metric queries), so we\n    55→\t// only send it when it's set\n    56→\tif query.MaxLines > 0 {\n    57→\t\tqs.Set(\"limit\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%d\", query.MaxLines))\n    58→\t}\n    59→\n    60→\tlokiUrl, err := url.Parse(lokiDsUrl)\n    61→\tif err != nil {\n    62→\t\treturn nil, backend.DownstreamError(fmt.Errorf(\"failed to parse Loki URL: %w\", err))\n    63→\t}\n    64→\n    65→\tswitch query.QueryType {\n    66→\tcase QueryTypeRange:\n    67→\t\t{\n    68→\t\t\tqs.Set(\"start\", strconv.FormatInt(query.Start.UnixNano(), 10))\n    69→\t\t\tqs.Set(\"end\", strconv.FormatInt(query.End.UnixNano(), 10))\n    70→\t\t\t// NOTE: technically for streams-producing queries `step`\n    71→\t\t\t// is ignored, so it would be nicer to not send it in such cases,\n    72→\t\t\t// but we cannot detect that situation, so we always send it.\n    73→\t\t\t// it should not break anything.\n    74→\t\t\t// NOTE2: we do this at millisecond precision for two reasons:\n    75→\t\t\t//  a. Loki cannot do steps with better precision anyway,\n    76→\t\t\t//     so the microsecond & nanosecond part can be ignored.\n    77→\t\t\t//  b. having it always be number+'ms' makes it more robust 85→\t\t\tqs.Set(\"time\", strconv.FormatInt(query.End.UnixNano(), 10))\n    86→\t\t\tlokiUrl.Path = path.Join(lokiUrl.Path, \"/loki/api/v1/query\")\n    87→\t\t}\n    88→\tdefault:\n    89→\t\treturn 97→\t}\n    98→\n    99→\tif query.SupportingQueryType != SupportingQueryNone {\n   100→\t\tvalue := getSupportingQueryHeaderValue(query.SupportingQueryType)\n   101→\t\tif value != \"\" {\n   102→\t\t\treq.Header.Set(\"X-Query-Tags\", \"Source=\"+value)\n   103→\t\t}\n   104→\t}\n   105→\treq.Header.Set(\"X-Loki-Response-Encoding-Flags\", \"categorize-labels\")\n   106→\tsetXScopeOrgIDHeader(req, ctx)\n   107→\n   108→\treturn req, nil\n   109→}\n   110→\n   111→type lokiResponseError struct {\n   112→\tMessage string `json:\"message\"`\n   113→\tTraceID string `json:\"traceID,omitempty\"`\n   114→}\n   115→\n   116→type lokiError struct {\n   117→\tMessage string\n   118→}\n   119→\n   120→func makeLokiError(bytes []byte) error {\n   121→\tvar data lokiError\n   122→\terr := json.Unmarshal(bytes, &data)\n   123→\tif err != nil {\n   124→\t\t// we were unable to convert the bytes to JSON, we return the whole text\n   125→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"%v\", string(bytes))\n   126→\t}\n   127→\n   128→\tif data.Message == \"\" {\n   129→\t\t// we got no usable error message, we return the whole text\n   130→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"%v\", string(bytes))\n   131→\t}\n   132→\n   133→\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"%v\", data.Message)\n   134→}\n   135→\n   136→// we know there is an error,\n   137→// based on the http-response-body\n   138→// we have to make an informative error-object\n   139→func readLokiError(body io.ReadCloser) error {\n   140→\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\n   141→\t_, err := buf.ReadFrom(body)\n   142→\tif err != nil {\n   143→\t\treturn err\n   144→\t}\n   145→\n   146→\tbytes := buf.Bytes()\n   147→\n   148→\t// the error-message is probably a JSON structure,\n   149→\t// with a string-field named \"message\". we want the\n   150→\t// value of that field.\n   151→\t// but, the response might be just a simple string,\n   152→\t// this was used in older Loki versions.\n   153→\t// so our approach is this:\n   154→\t// - we try to convert the bytes to JSON\n   155→\t// - we take the value of the field \"message\"\n   156→\t// - if any of these steps fail, or if \"message\" is empty, we return the whole text\n   157→\n   158→\treturn makeLokiError(bytes)\n   159→}\n   160→\n   161→func (api *LokiAPI) DataQuery(ctx context.Context, query lokiQuery, responseOpts ResponseOpts) (*backend.DataResponse, 204→\t\tapi.log.Debug(\"Error received from Loki\", lp...)\n   205→\t\treturn &res, nil\n   206→\t} else {\n   207→\t\tlp = append(lp, \"status\", \"ok\")\n   208→\t\tapi.log.Info(\"Response received 219→\t\tspan.RecordError(res.Error)\n   220→\t\tspan.SetStatus(codes.Error, res.Error.Error())\n   221→\t\tinstrumentation.UpdatePluginParsingResponseDurationSeconds(ctx, time.Since(start), RawQuery(ctx context.Context, resourcePath string) (RawLokiResponse, error) {\n   258→\tapi.log.Debug(\"Sending raw query to loki\", \"resourcePath\", resourcePath)\n   259→\treq, err := makeRawRequest(ctx, api.url, resourcePath)\n   260→\tif err != nil {\n   261→\t\tapi.log.Debug(\"Failed to prepare request to loki\", \"error\", err, \"resourcePath\", resourcePath)\n   262→\t\treturn RawLokiResponse{}, err\n   263→\t}\n   264→\tstart := time.Now()\n   265→\tresp, err := api.client.Do(req)\n   266→\tif err != nil {\n   267→\t\tstatus := \"error\"\n   268→\t\tif errors.Is(err, context.Canceled) {\n   269→\t\t\tstatus = \"cancelled\"\n   270→\t\t}\n   271→\t\tlp := []any{\"error\", err, \"resourcePath\", resourcePath, \"status\", status, \"duration\", time.Since(start), \"stage\", stageDatabaseRequest}\n   272→\t\tif resp != nil {\n   273→\t\t\tlp = append(lp, \"statusCode\", resp.StatusCode)\n   274→\t\t}\n   275→\t\tapi.log.Debug(\"Error received from Loki\", lp...)\n   276→\t\treturn RawLokiResponse{}, err\n   277→\t}\n   278→\n   279→\tdefer func() {\n   280→\t\tif err := resp.Body.Close(); err != nil {\n   281→\t\t\tapi.log.Warn(\"Failed to close response body\", \"error\", err)\n   282→\t\t}\n   283→\t}()\n   284→\n   285→\tapi.log.Info(\"Response received from loki\", \"status\", \"ok\", \"statusCode\", resp.StatusCode, \"contentLength\", resp.Header.Get(\"Content-Length\"), \"duration\", time.Since(start), \"contentEncoding\", resp.Header.Get(\"Content-Encoding\"), \"stage\", stageDatabaseRequest)\n   286→\n   287→\t// server errors are handled by the plugin-proxy to hide the error message\n   288→\tif resp.StatusCode/100 == 5 {\n   289→\t\treturn RawLokiResponse{}, readLokiError(resp.Body)\n   290→\t}\n   291→\n   292→\tbody,   298→\t// client errors are passed as a json struct to the client\n   299→\tif resp.StatusCode/100 != 2 {\n   300→\t\tlokiResponseErr := lokiResponseError{Message: makeLokiError(body).Error()}\n   301→\t\tapi.log.Warn(\"Non 200 HTTP status received from loki\", \"error\", lokiResponseErr.Message, \"statusCode\", resp.StatusCode, \"resourcePath\", resourcePath)\n   302→\t\ttraceID := 307→\t\tif err != nil {\n   308→\t\t\treturn RawLokiResponse{}, err\n   309→\t\t}\n   310→\t}\n   311→\n   312→\trawLokiResponse := RawLokiResponse{\n   313→\t\tBody:     body,\n   314→\t\tStatus:   resp.StatusCode,\n   315→\t\tEncoding: resp.Header.Get(\"Content-Encoding\"),\n   316→\t}\n   317→\n   318→\treturn rawLokiResponse, nil\n   319→}\n   320→\n   321→func getSupportingQueryHeaderValue(supportingQueryType SupportingQueryType) string {\n   322→\tvalue := \"\"\n   323→\n   324→\t// we need to map the SupportingQueryType to the actual header value.
